# e_lemma.txt (ver.2 for wordsmith 4) 


# compiled by yasumasa someya, september 1, 1998.


# this lemma list is provided "as is" and is free to use for any research


# and/or educational purposes. 


# the list currently contains 40,569 words (tokens) in 14,762 lemma groups. 


# it is still far from complete, but i hope you find the list useful in 


# preparing your own more complete lemma list. if you have any questions or


# comments about this lemma list, feel free to contact me (ysomeya@gol.com)


# at any time.


# note 1: you may want to change or delete some of the following entries:


#   'nt -> 't,nt,t


#   have -> has,having,had,'d,'ve,d,ve 


#   be -> am,are,is,was,were,being,been,'m,m


#   will -> 'll,ll


#   meet -> meets,met


#   meeting -> meetings


#   misunderstand -> misunderstands,misunderstood


#   misunderstanding -> misunderstandings


#   understand -> understands,understood


#   understanding -> understandings


# note 2: acronyms and other abbreviated words are listed here without


#   full stops.(e.g. ba, mr, messrs, tue, ymca, etc.)


# ==========================================================================
